                        "import unittest\nfrom unittest import mock\nimport sys\nimport tempfile\nimport subprocess\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# Import the code under test.\n# For the purpose of this test file, we assume all functions are available in the current namespace.\n# In practice, you would import them from the module, e.g.:\n# from installer_script import *\n\n# Copy-paste the functions here for test discovery (or assume they are imported)\n# For brevity, only import the functions to be tested if possible\n\n# The following are the functions to test:\n# - is_admin\n# - run_command\n# - download_python_installer\n# - install_python\n# - set_env_var\n# - verify_python_install\n# - install_dependencies\n# - compile_to_exe\n# - test_executable\n# - test_across_users\n\n# Since the code refers to PYTHON_INSTALL_DIR, etc., we need to define them for the test context\n\nPYTHON_VERSION = \"3.10.12\"\nPYTHON_ARCH = \"amd64\"\nPYTHON_INSTALL_DIR = Path(tempfile.gettempdir()) / \"Python310\"\nSOURCE_SCRIPT = Path(tempfile.gettempdir()) / \"your_script.py\"\nEXE_OUTPUT_DIR = Path(tempfile.gettempdir()) / \"dist\"\nDEPENDENCIES = [\"requests\", \"numpy\"]\nUSE_PYINSTALLER = True\n\n# Re-import the functions for test context\nimport types\n\ndef is_admin():\n    try:\n        return ctypes.windll.shell32.IsUserAnAdmin()\n    except Exception:\n        return False\n\ndef run_command(cmd, check=True, env=None):\n    print(f\"Running: {' '.join(cmd) if isinstance(cmd, list) else cmd}\")\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, check=check, shell=isinstance(cmd, str), env=env)\n    return result.returncode == 0\n\ndef download_python_installer(version, arch, out_path):\n    import urllib.request\n    base_url = f\"https://www.python.org/ftp/python/{version}/python-{version}-amd64.exe\" if arch == \"amd64\" else f\"https://www.python.org/ftp/python/{version}/python-{version}.exe\"\n    print(f\"Downloading Python installer from {base_url}...\")\n    urllib.request.urlretrieve(base_url, out_path)\n    print(f\"Downloaded to {out_path}\")\n\ndef install_python(installer_path, target_dir):\n    print(f\"Installing Python to {target_dir} ...\")\n    cmd = [\n        installer_path,\n        \"/quiet\",\n        f\"InstallAllUsers=1\",\n        f\"TargetDir={str(target_dir)}\",\n        \"PrependPath=1\",\n        \"Include_pip=1\"\n    ]\n    run_command(cmd)\n\ndef set_env_var(name, value, scope=\"USER\"):\n    print(f\"Setting environment variable: {name}={value} (Scope: {scope})\")\n    if scope == \"USER\":\n        subprocess.run(f'setx {name} \"{value}\"', shell=True)\n    elif scope == \"SYSTEM\":\n        if not is_admin():\n            print(\"System environment variable requires admin privileges!\")\n            return\n        subprocess.run(f'setx {name} \"{value}\" /M', shell=True)\n\ndef verify_python_install(python_exe):\n    print(f\"Verifying Python at {python_exe} ...\")\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_output([python_exe, \"--version\"])\n        return True\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Verification failed: {e}\")\n        return False\n\ndef install_dependencies(python_exe, packages):\n    print(f\"Installing dependencies: {packages}\")\n    for pkg in packages:\n        run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", pkg])\n\ndef compile_to_exe(python_exe, script_path, output_dir, use_pyinstaller=True):\n    if use_pyinstaller:\n        run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", \"pyinstaller\"])\n        cmd = [\n            python_exe, \"-m\", \"PyInstaller\",\n            \"--onefile\",\n            \"--distpath\", str(output_dir),\n            str(script_path)\n        ]\n        run_command(cmd)\n    else:\n        run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", \"cx_Freeze\"])\n        setup_code = f\"\"\"\nfrom cx_Freeze import onefile, Executable\n\nsetup(\n    name=\"App\",\n    version=\"1.0\",\n    description=\"Standalone App\",\n    executables=[Executable(\"{script_path}\", base=None)]\n)\n\"\"\"\n        setup_py = output_dir / \"setup.py\"\n        with open(setup_py, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(setup_code)\n        run_command([python_exe, str(setup_py), \"build\"])\n\ndef test_executable(exe_path):\n    print(f\"Testing executable: {exe_path}\")\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run([exe_path], capture_output=True, timeout=10)\n        print(\"Output:\")\n        print(result.stdout.decode(\"utf-8\"))\n        if result.returncode == 0:\n            print(\"Executable ran successfully.\")\n            return True\n        else:\n            print(f\"Executable exited with code {result.returncode}\")\n            return False\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to run executable: {e}\")\n        return False\n\ndef test_across_users(exe_path):\n    print(\"Testing across multiple user accounts (simulated)...\")\n    orig_home = os.environ.get(\"USERPROFILE\")\n    for test_user in [\"UserA\", \"UserB\"]:\n        print(f\"Simulating for user: {test_user}\")\n        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as temp_home:\n            os.environ[\"USERPROFILE\"] = temp_home\n            test_executable(exe_path)\n    if orig_home:\n        os.environ[\"USERPROFILE\"] = orig_home\n\n# Begin unittest suite\n\nclass TestPythonInstallerScript(unittest.TestCase):\n    @mock.patch(\"ctypes.windll.shell32.IsUserAnAdmin\", return_value=True)\n    def test_is_admin_true(self, mock_admin):\n        self.assertTrue(is_admin())\n\n    @mock.patch(\"ctypes.windll.shell32.IsUserAnAdmin\", side_effect=Exception(\"No admin\"))\n    def test_is_admin_exception(self, mock_admin):\n        self.assertFalse(is_admin())\n\n    @mock.patch(\"subprocess.run\")\n    def test_run_command_success(self, mock_run):\n        mock_run.return_value = mock.Mock(returncode=0)\n        self.assertTrue(run_command([\"echo\", \"hello\"]))\n\n    @mock.patch(\"subprocess.run\")\n    def test_run_command_failure(self, mock_run):\n        mock_run.return_value = mock.Mock(returncode=1)\n                         "import unittest\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport subprocess\nimport types\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# Import the functions from the provided code.\n# For the purpose of this test suite, we assume all functions are in a module named 'installer_script'.\n# If you save the code as 'installer_script.py', you can import as below.\n# Otherwise, copy the functions here or adjust the import as needed.\n\n# For demonstration, let's assume the functions are available in the global namespace.\n\n# We'll mock some system-level functions to avoid actual installations and modifications.\n\nimport builtins\n\nclass InstallerScriptTestSuite(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Setup temp directories and files for testing\n        self.temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        self.temp_script = Path(self.temp_dir) / \"test_script.py\"\n        self.temp_output_dir = Path(self.temp_dir) / \"dist\"\n        self.temp_output_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        with open(self.temp_script, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(\"print('Hello World')\")\n\n        # Patch environment variables\n        self.orig_environ = os.environ.copy()\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        # Clean up temp files and restore environment\n        shutil.rmtree(self.temp_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n        os.environ.clear()\n        os.environ.update(self.orig_environ)\n\n    def test_is_admin(self):\n        # Should construct correct URL for both archs\n        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=True) as tmp:\n            # We'll mock urllib.request.urlretrieve to avoid actual download\n            import urllib.request\n            orig_urlretrieve = urllib.request.urlretrieve\n\n            called = {}\n            def fake_urlretrieve(url, out_path):\n                called['url'] = url\n                called['out_path'] = out_path\n                with open(out_path, \"wb\") as f:\n                    f.write(b\"FAKE\")\n            urllib.request.urlretrieve = fake_urlretrieve\n\n            download_python_installer(\"3.10.12\", \"amd64\", tmp.name)\n            self.assertIn(\"amd64\", called['url'])\n            download_python_installer(\"3.10.12\", \"win32\", tmp.name)\n            self.assertNotIn(\"amd64\", called['url'])\n\n            urllib.request.urlretrieve = orig_urlretrieve\n\n    def test_set_env_var_user(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport sys\nimport subprocess\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport ctypes\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# --------------------- Configuration ---------------------\nPYTHON_VERSION = \"3.10.12\"\nPYTHON_ARCH = \"amd64\"  # \"amd64\" for 64-bit, \"win32\" for 32-bit\nPYTHON_INSTALL_DIR = Path(\"C:/Python310\")  # Change as needed\nSOURCE_SCRIPT = Path(\"your_script.py\")     # Change to your Python script\nEXE_OUTPUT_DIR = Path(\"dist\")\nDEPENDENCIES = [\"requests\", \"numpy\"]       # Add your dependencies here\nUSE_PYINSTALLER = True                     # Set False to use cx_Freeze\n\n# --------------------- Helper Functions ---------------------\n\ndef is_admin():\n    \"\"\"Check if running as admin (required for some operations).\"\"\"\n    try:\n        return ctypes.windll.shell32.IsUserAnAdmin()\n    except Exception:\n        return False\n\ndef run_command(cmd, check=True, env=None, capture_output=False, timeout=None, cwd=None):\n    \"\"\"Run a shell command and return CompletedProcess.\"\"\"\n    if isinstance(cmd, list):\n        print(f\"Running: {' '.join(str(c) for c in cmd)}\")\n    else:\n        print(f\"Running: {cmd}\")\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(\n            cmd,\n            check=check,\n            shell=isinstance(cmd, str),\n            env=env,\n            capture_output=capture_output,\n            timeout=timeout,\n            cwd=cwd\n        )\n        return result\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        print(f\"Command failed: {e}\")\n        if e.stdout:\n            print(e.stdout.decode(errors=\"ignore\"))\n        if e.stderr:\n            print(e.stderr.decode(errors=\"ignore\"))\n        return None\n\ndef download_python_installer(version, arch, out_path):\n    \"\"\"Download official Python installer.\"\"\"\n    import urllib.request\n    if arch == \"amd64\":\n        base_url = f\"https://www.python.org/ftp/python/{version}/python-{version}-amd64.exe\"\n    else:\n        base_url = f\"https://www.python.org/ftp/python/{version}/python-{version}.exe\"\n target_dir):\n    \"\"\"Install Python silently.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"Installing Python to {target_dir} ...\")\n    cmd = [\n        str(installer_path),\n        \"/quiet\",\n        \"InstallAllUsers=1\",\n        f\"TargetDir={str(target_dir)}\",\n        \"PrependPath=1\",\n        \"Include_pip=1\"\n    ]\n    result = run_command(cmd, check=False)\n    if result is None or result.returncode != 0:\n        print(\"Python installer failed. You may need to run as Administrator.\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\ndef set_env_var(name, value, scope=\"USER\"):\n    \"\"\"Set environment variable (USER or SYSTEM).\"\"\"\n    print(f\"Setting environment variable: {name}={value} (Scope: {scope})\")\n    if scope == \"USER\":\n        subprocess.run(f'setx {name} \"{value}\"', shell=True)\n    elif scope == \"SYSTEM\":\n        if not is_admin():\n            print(\"System environment variable requires admin privileges!\")\n            return\n        subprocess.run(f'setx {name} \"{value}\" /M', shell=True)\n\ndef verify_python_install(python_exe):\n    \"\"\"Verify Python installation.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"Verifying Python at {python_exe} ...\")\n    try:\n        out = subprocess.check_output([python_exe, \"--version\"], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)\n        print(out.decode().strip())\n        return True\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Verification failed: {e}\")\n        return False\n\ndef install_dependencies(python_exe, packages):\n    \"\"\"Install required packages using pip.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"Installing dependencies: {packages}\")\n    # Ensure pip is up to date\n    run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", \"--upgrade\", \"pip\"], check=False)\n    for pkg in packages:\n        result = run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", pkg], check=False)\n        if result is None or result.returncode != 0:\n            print(f\"Failed to install dependency: {pkg}\")\n            sys.exit(1)\n\ndef compile_to_exe(python_exe, script_path, output_dir, use_pyinstaller=True):\n    \"\"\"Compile Python script to .exe using PyInstaller or cx_Freeze.\"\"\"\n    if use_pyinstaller:\n        print(\"Using PyInstaller to compile executable...\")\n        run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", \"--upgrade\", \"pyinstaller\"], check=False)\n        # Remove previous build if exists\n        build_dir = output_dir.parent / \"build\"\n        if build_dir.exists():\n            shutil.rmtree(build_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n        if output_dir.exists():\n            shutil.rmtree(output_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n        cmd = [\n            python_exe, \"-m\", \"PyInstaller\",\n            \"--onefile\",\n            \"--distpath\", str(output_dir),\n            \"--workpath\", str(build_dir),\n            \"--clean\",\n            str(script_path)\n        ]\n        result = run_command(cmd, check=False)\n        if result is None or result.returncode != 0:\n            print(\"PyInstaller failed to create executable.\")\n            sys.exit(1)\n    else:\n        print(\"Using cx_Freeze to compile executable...\")\n        run_command([python_exe, \"-m\", \"pip\", \"install\", \"--upgrade\", \"cx_Freeze\"], check=False)\n        # Remove previous build if exists\n        build_dir = output_dir / \"build\"\n        if build_dir.exists():\n            shutil.rmtree(build_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n        result = run_command([python_exe, str(setup_py), \"build\"], check=False, cwd=str(output_dir))\n        if result is None or result.returncode != 0:\n            print(\"cx_Freeze failed to create executable.\")\n            sys.exit(1)\n\ndef locate_executable(output_dir, script_name):\n    \"\"\"Locate the generated .exe file.\"\"\"\n    exe_name = script_name + \".exe\"\n    # self.assertIn(\"sys.exit called\", str(cm.exception))\n\n    def test_locate_executable_in_dist(self):\n        # Should find exe directly in output_dir\n        exe =
